 Also, CNG buses and other eco friendly vehicles are also being run in Delhi
 iske baavjood dilli desh kaa sabase zyada pradooshan vaala shahar he
 According to a recent study by the Ministry of Science and Technology, Delhi's environment is extremely dangerous in terms of health
 dilli kii phija main outdoor particulate matter (piem) kii maatra saamaanya se kahin zyada he
 "the pollution in Delhi has increased by 21% in the last ten years and continues to grow," said Sagnik De k Mutabik, Assistant Professor at the Center for Atmospheric Sciences, IIT Delhi
 dilli ke vaataavaran main din ke 50 fisadi se bhi adhik samay main pradooshan kii maatra bahut zyada hoti he
 This pollution is so dangerous that it can cause respiratory, heart and other serious diseases
 adhyayan se pataa chalaa he ki dilli ke alaava meerut, kanpur, agra, patna, kolkata or mumbaibhi pradooshan kii vajah se khatarnaak hota ja rahaa he
 The purpose of this study is to find out the amount of pollution and its side effects in rural and urban areas so that a national health database can be created
 adhyayan main bataaya gaya he ki piem (particulate matter) 2
 The volume of 5 size particles is increasing rapidly which can go very deep in the respiratory system
 gauratlab he ki hawa main maujuud ve kan jo saans ke saath andar ja sakate hai, unhen particulate matter (piem) kaha jaataa he
 Scientists from IIT Delhi, IIT Kanpur, University of Illinois and US & Dalhousie University of Canada participated in this research
 vaigyanikon ne remote sencing takanic kii madad se pradooshan ke lihaaj se bharat main 5 bade jone kaa bhi pataa lagaaya

 kuch din pehle hi jawaharlal nehru uniwarsity ke ekaresearch main bhi kaha gaya he ki dilli kii phija cancer paidaa karne vaale kanon se bhari hui he

 If Article 356 of the Indian Constitution is defined in simple language, then it is called President's rule
 yah shashan haal main uttarakhand main laga he
 Under this article, the state government is dismissed and the power of the state goes to the governor instead of the state government
 bataa den ki governor kii niyukti raashtrapati dwaara hoti he
 After the implementation of article 356, the Chief Minister's chair in the state becomes vacant and the Cabinet Group cannot do any work
 haalanki is artical kaa hamaare desh main upyog kam or durupyog zyada hua he
 The government at the center uses this article to periodically harass the opposition parties
 raashtrapati shashan (artical 356) lagane kii sharten
 
 
 - The assembly of the state is unable to elect its chief minister - the collapse of the coalition - the lack of majority in the assembly - the absence of elections due to any unavoidable reasons - until the 90s it was often seen that the central governments with the help of the governor Used to create conditions
 haalanki san 1994 main ucchtam nyaayalay ke ek faisle ke baad iskaa anuchit istemaal kam ho gaya
 Where is the President's rule so far - Uttarakhand has seen 7 Chief Ministers in 15 years of its creation
 - avibhajit uttarapradesh ab tak 9 baar raashtrapati shashan kaa dansh jhel chukaa he
 - So far, President's rule has been imposed 123 times in different states and union territories
 in rajyon main itani baar lagaahai raashtrapati shashan-andhra pradesh: 2arunachal pradesh: 4assam: 4bihar: 8dilli: 1goa: 5gujarat: 5haryana: 3himachal pradesh: 2jammu kashmir: 6jharkhand: 3karnataka: 6kerala: 4madhya pradesh: 3maharashtra: 2manipur: 10meghalaya: 2mizoram: 3nagaland: 4urisa: 6puducheri: 6punjab: 8rajasthan: 4sikkim: 2tamilnadu: 4tripura: 3uttar pradesh: 9pashchim bengal: 4ye tathy bhi jaane--jammu kashmir main adhiktam raashtrapati shashan 6 saal 264 din chalaa he to vahiin nunatam karnataka rajya main 7 dinon ke liye chalaa he
